(** instantiates the scheme from [GenMendlerIteration_alt] for use in the analysis of recursion schemes involving
    actegories (hence, with actions of monoidal categories on categories)

author: Ralph Matthes, 2023
*)

Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

Import BifunctorNotations.

Section FixAnActegory.

  Context {V : category} (Mon_V : monoidal V) {C : category}
    (IC : Initial C) (CC : Colims_of_shape nat_graph C)
    (Act : actegory Mon_V C)
    (v : V).

Section FixAFunctor.

  Context (F : functor C C) (HF : is_omega_cocont F).

  Let AF : category := FunctorAlg F.
  Let chnF : chain C := initChain IC F.
  Let μF_Initial : Initial AF := colimAlgInitial IC HF (CC chnF).
  Let μF : C := alg_carrier _ (InitialObject μF_Initial).
  Let α : F μF --> μF := alg_map F (pr1 μF_Initial).

  Context (y : C) (G : functor C C) (ρ' : G y --> y).

  Let L : functor C C := leftwhiskering_functor Act v.

  Context (IL : isInitial C (v ⊗_{Act} (InitialObject IC))) (HL : is_omega_cocont L).

  Definition SpecialGenMendlerIterationWithActegory (θ' : F ∙ L ⟹ L ∙ G) :
    ∃! h : v ⊗_{Act} μF --> y, v ⊗^{Act}_{l} α · h = θ' μF · #G h · ρ'
    := SpecialGenMendlerIteration IC CC F HF y L IL HL G ρ' θ'.

End FixAFunctor.

Section Const_H_AsFunctor.

  Context (CP : BinCoproducts C).

  Context (H : functor C C) (HH : is_omega_cocont H) (c0 : C).

  Let Const_plus_H (c : C) : functor C C := GeneralizedSubstitutionSystems.Const_plus_H H CP c.

  Let AF : category := FunctorAlg (Const_plus_H c0).
  Let chnF : chain C := initChain IC (Const_plus_H c0).

  Qed.

  Let μF_Initial : Initial AF := colimAlgInitial IC HF (CC chnF).
  Let μF : C := alg_carrier _ (InitialObject μF_Initial).
  Let α : Const_plus_H c0 μF --> μF := alg_map (Const_plus_H c0) (pr1 μF_Initial).

  Let η : constant_functor C C c0 μF --> μF := BinCoproductIn1 (CP _ _) · α.
  Let τ : H μF --> μF := BinCoproductIn2 (CP _ _) · α.

  Context (y : C) (θ : lineator_lax Mon_V Act Act H) (ρ : H y --> y) (f : v ⊗_{Act} c0 --> y).

  Context (IL : isInitial C (v ⊗_{Act} (InitialObject IC))).

  Let L : functor C C := leftwhiskering_functor Act v.

  Context (HL : is_omega_cocont L).


  Definition charprop_SpecialGenMendlerIterationWithActegoryAndStrength (h : C ⟦v ⊗_{Act} μF, y⟧) : UU :=
    v ⊗^{Act}_{l} η · h = f × v ⊗^{Act}_{l} τ · h = θ v μF · #H h · ρ.

α:= alg_map (Const_plus_H c0) (pr1 μF_Initial): C ⟦ Const_plus_H c0 μF, μF ⟧
η:= BinCoproductIn1
  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ constant_functor C C c0 μF, μF ⟧

  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ H μF, μF ⟧
y: C

isaprop
  (charprop_SpecialGenMendlerIterationWithActegoryAndStrength
     h)

    apply isapropdirprod; apply C.
  Qed.

  Definition singleeq_SpecialGenMendlerIterationWithActegoryAndStrength (h : C ⟦v ⊗_{Act} μF, y⟧) : UU :=
    actegory_bincoprod_antidistributor Mon_V CP Act _ _ _ · v ⊗^{Act}_{l} α · h =
                                     BinCoproductArrow (CP _ _) f (θ v μF · #H h · ρ).

  Context (δ : actegory_bincoprod_distributor Mon_V CP Act).

  Definition instance_SpecialGenMendlerIterationWithActegory (h : C ⟦v ⊗_{Act} μF, y⟧) : UU :=
    v ⊗^{Act}_{l} α · h = δ v c0 (H μF) · BinCoproductOfArrows _ (CP _ _) (CP _ _) f (θ v μF) ·
                            #(Const_plus_H y) h · BinCoproductArrow (CP _ _) (identity y) ρ.

actegory_bincoprod_antidistributor Mon_V CP Act v
  (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)
· v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} α · h =
BinCoproductArrow
  (CP (v ⊗_{ Act} c0) (v ⊗_{ Act} H μF)) f
  (θ v μF · # H h · ρ)

      
V: category
Mon_V: monoidal V
C: category
IC: Initial C
CC: Colims_of_shape nat_graph C
Act: actegory Mon_V C
v: V
CP: BinCoproducts C
H: C ⟶ C
HH: is_omega_cocont H
c0: C
Const_plus_H:= λ c : C,
GeneralizedSubstitutionSystems.Const_plus_H
  H CP c: C → C ⟶ C
AF:= FunctorAlg (Const_plus_H c0): category
chnF:= initChain IC (Const_plus_H c0): chain C
μF_Initial:= colimAlgInitial IC HF (CC chnF): Initial AF
μF:= alg_carrier (Const_plus_H c0) μF_Initial: C
α:= alg_map (Const_plus_H c0) (pr1 μF_Initial): C ⟦ Const_plus_H c0 μF, μF ⟧
η:= BinCoproductIn1
  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ constant_functor C C c0 μF, μF ⟧
τ:= BinCoproductIn2
  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ H μF, μF ⟧
y: C
θ: lineator_lax Mon_V Act Act H
ρ: C ⟦ H y, y ⟧
f: C ⟦ v ⊗_{ Act} c0, y ⟧
IL: isInitial C (v ⊗_{ Act} IC)
L:= leftwhiskering_functor Act v: C ⟶ C
HL: is_omega_cocont L
δ: actegory_bincoprod_distributor Mon_V CP Act
h: C ⟦ v ⊗_{ Act} μF, y ⟧
Hchar1: v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} η · h = f
Hchar2: v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} τ · h = θ v μF · # H h · ρ
BinCoproductIn1
  (CP
     (leftwhiskering_functor Act v
        (constant_functor C C c0 μF))
     (leftwhiskering_functor Act v (H μF)))
· (actegory_bincoprod_antidistributor Mon_V CP Act v
     (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)
   · v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} α · h) =
BinCoproductIn1
  (CP
     (leftwhiskering_functor Act v
        (constant_functor C C c0 μF))
     (leftwhiskering_functor Act v (H μF)))
· BinCoproductArrow
    (CP (v ⊗_{ Act} c0) (v ⊗_{ Act} H μF)) f
    (θ v μF · # H h · ρ)

          apply BinCoproductIn2Commutes. 
V: category
Mon_V: monoidal V
C: category
IC: Initial C
CC: Colims_of_shape nat_graph C
Act: actegory Mon_V C
v: V
CP: BinCoproducts C
H: C ⟶ C
HH: is_omega_cocont H
c0: C
Const_plus_H:= λ c : C,
GeneralizedSubstitutionSystems.Const_plus_H
  H CP c: C → C ⟶ C
AF:= FunctorAlg (Const_plus_H c0): category
chnF:= initChain IC (Const_plus_H c0): chain C
μF_Initial:= colimAlgInitial IC HF (CC chnF): Initial AF
μF:= alg_carrier (Const_plus_H c0) μF_Initial: C
α:= alg_map (Const_plus_H c0) (pr1 μF_Initial): C ⟦ Const_plus_H c0 μF, μF ⟧
η:= BinCoproductIn1
  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ constant_functor C C c0 μF, μF ⟧
τ:= BinCoproductIn2
  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ H μF, μF ⟧
y: C
θ: lineator_lax Mon_V Act Act H
ρ: C ⟦ H y, y ⟧
f: C ⟦ v ⊗_{ Act} c0, y ⟧
IL: isInitial C (v ⊗_{ Act} IC)
L:= leftwhiskering_functor Act v: C ⟶ C
HL: is_omega_cocont L
δ: actegory_bincoprod_distributor Mon_V CP Act
h: C ⟦ v ⊗_{ Act} μF, y ⟧
Hchar1: v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} η · h = f
Hchar2: v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} τ · h = θ v μF · # H h · ρ
# (leftwhiskering_functor Act v)
  (BinCoproductIn2
     (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)))
· v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} α · h =
BinCoproductIn2
  (CP
     (leftwhiskering_functor Act v
        (constant_functor C C c0 μF))
     (leftwhiskering_functor Act v (H μF)))
· BinCoproductArrow
    (CP (v ⊗_{ Act} c0) (v ⊗_{ Act} H μF)) f
    (θ v μF · # H h · ρ)

  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ constant_functor C C c0 μF, μF ⟧
τ:= BinCoproductIn2
  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ H μF, μF ⟧
y: C
θ: lineator_lax Mon_V Act Act H
ρ: C ⟦ H y, y ⟧
f: C ⟦ v ⊗_{ Act} c0, y ⟧
IL: isInitial C (v ⊗_{ Act} IC)
L:= leftwhiskering_functor Act v: C ⟶ C
HL: is_omega_cocont L
δ: actegory_bincoprod_distributor Mon_V CP Act
h: C ⟦ v ⊗_{ Act} μF, y ⟧
Hsingle: # (leftwhiskering_functor Act v)
  (BinCoproductIn1
     (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)))
· v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} α · h =
BinCoproductIn1
  (CP
     (leftwhiskering_functor Act v
        (constant_functor C C c0 μF))
     (leftwhiskering_functor Act v (H μF)))
· BinCoproductArrow
    (CP (v ⊗_{ Act} c0) (v ⊗_{ Act} H μF)) f
    (θ v μF · # H h · ρ)
aux: v
⊗^{ Act}_{l} (BinCoproductIn1
                (CP c0 (H (colim (CC chnF))))
              · colim_algebra_mor IC HF
                  (CC chnF)) · h =
v
⊗^{ Act}_{l} BinCoproductIn1
               (CP c0 (H (colim (CC chnF))))
· v
  ⊗^{ Act}_{l} colim_algebra_mor IC HF (CC chnF)
· h
Hsingle': v
⊗^{ Act}_{l} (BinCoproductIn1
                (CP c0
                   (H (colim (CC chnF))))
              · colim_algebra_mor IC HF
                  (CC chnF)) · h =
BinCoproductIn1
  (CP
     (leftwhiskering_functor Act v
        (constant_functor C C c0 μF))
     (leftwhiskering_functor Act v (H μF)))
· BinCoproductArrow
    (CP (v ⊗_{ Act} c0) (v ⊗_{ Act} H μF))
    f (θ v μF · # H h · ρ)
v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} η · h = f

Hsingle: # (leftwhiskering_functor Act v)
  (BinCoproductIn2
     (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)))
· v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} α · h =
BinCoproductIn2
  (CP
     (leftwhiskering_functor Act v
        (constant_functor C C c0 μF))
     (leftwhiskering_functor Act v (H μF)))
· BinCoproductArrow
    (CP (v ⊗_{ Act} c0) (v ⊗_{ Act} H μF)) f
    (θ v μF · # H h · ρ)
aux: v
⊗^{ Act}_{l} (BinCoproductIn2
                (CP c0 (H (colim (CC chnF))))
              · colim_algebra_mor IC HF
                  (CC chnF)) · h =
v
⊗^{ Act}_{l} BinCoproductIn2
               (CP c0 (H (colim (CC chnF))))
· v
  ⊗^{ Act}_{l} colim_algebra_mor IC HF (CC chnF)
· h
v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} τ · h = θ v μF · # H h · ρ

  H CP c: C → C ⟶ C

  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ constant_functor C C c0 μF, μF ⟧
τ:= BinCoproductIn2
  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ H μF, μF ⟧
y: C
θ: lineator_lax Mon_V Act Act H
ρ: C ⟦ H y, y ⟧
f: C ⟦ v ⊗_{ Act} c0, y ⟧
IL: isInitial C (v ⊗_{ Act} IC)
L:= leftwhiskering_functor Act v: C ⟶ C
HL: is_omega_cocont L

· (v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} α · h) =

  (CP (v ⊗_{ Act} c0) (v ⊗_{ Act} H μF)) f
  (θ v μF · # H h · ρ)

Mon_V: monoidal V
C: category
IC: Initial C
CC: Colims_of_shape nat_graph C
Act: actegory Mon_V C
v: V
CP: BinCoproducts C
H: C ⟶ C
HH: is_omega_cocont H
c0: C
Const_plus_H:= λ c : C,
GeneralizedSubstitutionSystems.Const_plus_H
  H CP c: C → C ⟶ C
AF:= FunctorAlg (Const_plus_H c0): category
chnF:= initChain IC (Const_plus_H c0): chain C
μF_Initial:= colimAlgInitial IC HF (CC chnF): Initial AF
μF:= alg_carrier (Const_plus_H c0) μF_Initial: C
α:= alg_map (Const_plus_H c0) (pr1 μF_Initial): C ⟦ Const_plus_H c0 μF, μF ⟧
η:= BinCoproductIn1
  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ constant_functor C C c0 μF, μF ⟧
τ:= BinCoproductIn2
  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ H μF, μF ⟧
y: C
θ: lineator_lax Mon_V Act Act H
ρ: C ⟦ H y, y ⟧
f: C ⟦ v ⊗_{ Act} c0, y ⟧
IL: isInitial C (v ⊗_{ Act} IC)
L:= leftwhiskering_functor Act v: C ⟶ C
HL: is_omega_cocont L
δ: actegory_bincoprod_distributor Mon_V CP Act
h: C ⟦ v ⊗_{ Act} μF, y ⟧
Hinst: v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} α · h =
δ v c0 (H μF)
· BinCoproductOfArrows C
    (CP (v ⊗_{ Act} c0) (v ⊗_{ Act} H μF))
    (CP y (H (v ⊗_{ Act} μF))) f 
    (θ v μF) · # (Const_plus_H y) h
· BinCoproductArrow (CP y (H y)) 
    (identity y) ρ
v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} α · h =
(bincoprod_functor_lineator_data Mon_V CP Act δ v
   (c0,, pr1 H μF),,
 bincoprod_functor_lineator_strongly Mon_V CP Act δ v
   (c0,, pr1 H μF))
· BinCoproductArrow
    (CP (v ⊗_{ Act} c0) (v ⊗_{ Act} H μF)) f
    (θ v μF · # H h · ρ)

y: C
θ: lineator_lax Mon_V Act Act H
ρ: C ⟦ H y, y ⟧
f: C ⟦ v ⊗_{ Act} c0, y ⟧
IL: isInitial C (v ⊗_{ Act} IC)
L:= leftwhiskering_functor Act v: C ⟶ C
HL: is_omega_cocont L
δ: actegory_bincoprod_distributor Mon_V CP Act
h: C ⟦ v ⊗_{ Act} μF, y ⟧
Hsingle: actegory_bincoprod_antidistributor Mon_V CP
  Act v (constant_functor C C c0 μF) 
  (H μF) · v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} α · h =
BinCoproductArrow
  (CP (v ⊗_{ Act} c0) (v ⊗_{ Act} H μF)) f
  (θ v μF · # H h · ρ)
v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} α · h =
δ v c0 (H μF)
· BinCoproductOfArrows C
    (CP (v ⊗_{ Act} c0) (v ⊗_{ Act} H μF))
    (CP y (H (v ⊗_{ Act} μF))) f (θ v μF)
· # (Const_plus_H y) h
· BinCoproductArrow (CP y (H y)) (identity y) ρ

τ:= BinCoproductIn2
  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ H μF, μF ⟧
y: C
θ: lineator_lax Mon_V Act Act H
ρ: C ⟦ H y, y ⟧
f: C ⟦ v ⊗_{ Act} c0, y ⟧
IL: isInitial C (v ⊗_{ Act} IC)
L:= leftwhiskering_functor Act v: C ⟶ C
HL: is_omega_cocont L
δ: actegory_bincoprod_distributor Mon_V CP Act
δll:= bincoprod_functor_lineator Mon_V CP Act δ: lineator Mon_V
  (ProductActegory.actegory_binprod Mon_V Act
     Act) Act (bincoproduct_functor CP)
is_nat_trans (Const_plus_H c0 ∙ L)
  (L ∙ Const_plus_H y) θ'_data

   · BinCoproduct_of_functors_mor C C CP
       (constant_functor C C y) H (v ⊗_{ Act} c)
       (v ⊗_{ Act} c') (v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} g))

  H CP c: C → C ⟶ C

  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ constant_functor C C c0 μF, μF ⟧

  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ H μF, μF ⟧

HL: is_omega_cocont L

  (ProductActegory.actegory_binprod Mon_V Act
     Act) Act (bincoproduct_functor CP)
c, c': C
g: C ⟦ c, c' ⟧
# (bincoproduct_functor CP)
  (v
   ⊗^{ ProductActegory.actegory_binprod Mon_V Act Act}_{l} 
   ((pr12 C) c0,, pr2 H c c' g))
· BinCoproductOfArrows C
    (CP (v ⊗_{ Act} c0) (v ⊗_{ Act} H c'))

HL: is_omega_cocont L
δ: actegory_bincoprod_distributor Mon_V CP Act
δll:= bincoprod_functor_lineator Mon_V CP Act δ: lineator Mon_V
  (ProductActegory.actegory_binprod Mon_V Act
     Act) Act (bincoproduct_functor CP)
c, c': C
g: C ⟦ c, c' ⟧
BinCoproductOfArrows C
  (CP (v ⊗_{ Act} c0) (v ⊗_{ Act} pr1 H c))
  (CP y (H (v ⊗_{ Act} c')))
  (v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} (pr12 C) c0 · f)
  (v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} pr2 H c c' g · θ v c') =
BinCoproductOfArrows C
  (CP (v ⊗_{ Act} c0) (v ⊗_{ Act} H c))
  (CP y (H (v ⊗_{ Act} c'))) (f · identity y)
  (θ v c · # H (v ⊗^{ Act}_{l} g))

c0: C

GeneralizedSubstitutionSystems.Const_plus_H
  H CP c: C → C ⟶ C

μF_Initial:= colimAlgInitial IC HF (CC chnF): Initial AF
μF:= alg_carrier (Const_plus_H c0) μF_Initial: C
α:= alg_map (Const_plus_H c0) (pr1 μF_Initial): C ⟦ Const_plus_H c0 μF, μF ⟧
η:= BinCoproductIn1
  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ constant_functor C C c0 μF, μF ⟧
τ:= BinCoproductIn2
  (CP (constant_functor C C c0 μF) (H μF)) · α: C ⟦ H μF, μF ⟧

f: C ⟦ v ⊗_{ Act} c0, y ⟧

HL: is_omega_cocont L
δ: actegory_bincoprod_distributor Mon_V CP Act

  (ProductActegory.actegory_binprod Mon_V Act
     Act) Act (bincoproduct_functor CP)

y0 : ∑ h : C ⟦ v ⊗_{ Act} μF, y ⟧,
     charprop_SpecialGenMendlerIterationWithActegoryAndStrength
       h, ?p (?s y0) = y0
